Answer in one short sentence.\",\n        role: \"user\",\n      },\n    ],\n  });\n\n  console.log(result);\n}\n\nrun();\n"} />

<ExpandableProperty
  slot="entry"
  id="frequency_penalty"
  headingId="operation-chat_completion_v1_chat_completions_post+request+frequency_penalty"
  typeInfo={{"label":"number","linkedLabel":"number","children":[],"breakoutSubTypes":{}}}
  typeAnnotations={[{"title":"Min: -2","variant":"warning"},{"title":"Max: 2","variant":"warning"}]}
  hasExpandableContent={true}
  expandByDefault={true}
>

<ExpandablePropertyTitle slot="title">

##### frequency_penalty \{#operation-chat_completion_v1_chat_completions_post+request+frequency_penalty\}

</ExpandablePropertyTitle>

<ExpandablePropertyDescription slot="description">

frequency_penalty penalizes the repetition of words based on their frequency in the generated text. A higher frequency penalty discourages the model from repeating words that have already appeared frequently in the output, promoting diversity and reducing repetition.

</ExpandablePropertyDescription>

<ExpandablePropertyExamples slot="examples">

<DebugPlaceholder>

No examples provided

_OpenAPI example:_

```
examples:
  - MyExampleValue
```

</DebugPlaceholder>

</ExpandablePropertyExamples>

<ExpandablePropertyDefaultValue slot="defaultValue">

_Default Value:_ `0`

</ExpandablePropertyDefaultValue>

</ExpandableProperty>

<ExpandableProperty
  slot="entry"
  id="max_tokens"
  headingId="operation-chat_completion_v1_chat_completions_post+request+max_tokens"
  typeInfo={{"label":"union","linkedLabel":"union","children":[{"label":"integer","linkedLabel":"integer","children":[],"breakoutSubTypes":{}},{"label":"null","linkedLabel":"null","children":[],"breakoutSubTypes":{}}],"breakoutSubTypes":{}}}
  typeAnnotations={[]}
  hasExpandableContent={true}
  expandByDefault={true}
>

<ExpandablePropertyTitle slot="title">

##### max_tokens \{#operation-chat_completion_v1_chat_completions_post+request+max_tokens\}

</ExpandablePropertyTitle>

<ExpandablePropertyDescription slot="description">

The maximum number of tokens to generate in the completion. The token count of your prompt plus `max_tokens` cannot exceed the model's context length.

</ExpandablePropertyDescription>

<DebugPlaceholder>

##### prefix \{#operation-chat_completion_v1_chat_completions_post+request+messages+assistantmessage+prefix\}

</ExpandablePropertyTitle>

<ExpandablePropertyDescription slot="description">

<ExpandablePropertyTitle slot="title">

##### presence_penalty \{#operation-chat_completion_v1_chat_completions_post+request+presence_penalty\}

</ExpandablePropertyTitle>

<ExpandablePropertyDescription slot="description">

presence_penalty determines how much the model penalizes the repetition of words or phrases. A higher presence penalty encourages the model to use a wider variety of words and phrases, making the output more diverse and creative.

</ExpandablePropertyDescription>

<ExpandablePropertyTitle slot="title">

##### type \{#operation-chat_completion_v1_chat_completions_post+request+response_format+responseformat+type\}

</ExpandablePropertyTitle>

<ExpandablePropertyDescription slot="description">

An object specifying the format that the model must output. Setting to `\{ "type": "json_object" \}` enables JSON mode, which guarantees the message the model generates is in JSON. When using JSON mode you MUST also instruct the model to produce JSON yourself with a system or a user message.

</ExpandablePropertyDescription>

<ExpandableProperty
  slot="entry"
  id="stream"
  headingId="operation-chat_completion_v1_chat_completions_post+request+stream"
  typeInfo={{"label":"boolean","linkedLabel":"boolean","children":[],"breakoutSubTypes":{}}}
  typeAnnotations={[]}
  hasExpandableContent={true}
  expandByDefault={true}
>

<ExpandablePropertyTitle slot="title">

##### stream \{#operation-chat_completion_v1_chat_completions_post+request+stream\}

</ExpandablePropertyTitle>

<ExpandablePropertyDescription slot="description">

Whether to stream back partial progress. If set, tokens will be sent as data-only server-side events as they become available, with the stream terminated by a data: [DONE] message. Otherwise, the server will hold the request open until the timeout or until completion, with the response containing the full result as JSON.

</ExpandablePropertyDescription>

<ExpandablePropertyExamples slot="examples">

<DebugPlaceholder>

No examples provided

_OpenAPI example:_

```
examples:
  - MyExampleValue
```

</DebugPlaceholder>

</ExpandablePropertyExamples>

<ExpandablePropertyDefaultValue slot="defaultValue">

_Default Value:_ `false`

</ExpandablePropertyDefaultValue>

</ExpandableProperty>

<ExpandableProperty
  slot="entry"
  id="temperature"
  headingId="operation-chat_completion_v1_chat_completions_post+request+temperature"
  typeInfo={{"label":"union","linkedLabel":"union","children":[{"label":"number","linkedLabel":"number","children":[],"breakoutSubTypes":{}},{"label":"null","linkedLabel":"null","children":[],"breakoutSubTypes":{}}],"breakoutSubTypes":{}}}
  typeAnnotations={[]}
  hasExpandableContent={true}
  expandByDefault={true}
>

<ExpandablePropertyTitle slot="title">

##### temperature \{#operation-chat_completion_v1_chat_completions_post+request+temperature\}

</ExpandablePropertyTitle>

<ExpandablePropertyDescription slot="description">

What sampling temperature to use, we recommend between 0.0 and 0.7. Higher values like 0.7 will make the output more random, while lower values like 0.2 will make it more focused and deterministic. We generally recommend altering this or `top_p` but not both. The default value varies depending on the model you are targeting. Call the `/models` endpoint to retrieve the appropriate value.

</ExpandablePropertyDescription>

<ExpandableProperty
  slot="entry"
  id="top_p"
  headingId="operation-chat_completion_v1_chat_completions_post+request+top_p"
  typeInfo={{"label":"number","linkedLabel":"number","children":[],"breakoutSubTypes":{}}}
  typeAnnotations={[{"title":"Min: 0","variant":"warning"},{"title":"Max: 1","variant":"warning"}]}
  hasExpandableContent={true}
  expandByDefault={true}
>

<ExpandablePropertyTitle slot="title">

##### top_p \{#operation-chat_completion_v1_chat_completions_post+request+top_p\}

</ExpandablePropertyTitle>

<ExpandablePropertyDescription slot="description">

Nucleus sampling, where the model considers the results of the tokens with `top_p` probability mass. So 0.1 means only the tokens comprising the top 10% probability mass are considered. We generally recommend altering this or `temperature` but not both.

</ExpandablePropertyDescription>

<ExpandablePropertyExamples slot="examples">

<DebugPlaceholder>

No examples provided

_OpenAPI example:_

```
examples:
  - MyExampleValue
```

</DebugPlaceholder>

</ExpandablePropertyExamples>

<ExpandablePropertyDefaultValue slot="defaultValue">

_Default Value:_ `1`

</ExpandablePropertyDefaultValue>

<ExpandablePropertyTitle slot="title">

##### prefix \{#operation-chat_completion_v1_chat_completions_post+responses+200+application-json+choices+chatcompletionchoice+message+assistantmessage+prefix\}

</ExpandablePropertyTitle>

<ExpandablePropertyDescription slot="description">

Set this to `true` when adding an assistant message as prefix to condition the model response. The role of the prefix message is to force the model to start its answer by the content of the message.

</ExpandablePropertyDescription>
